	generic_gen_4_light_upgrade = {
		icon = GFX_decision_t90_button

		days_remove = -1
		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			#has_air_experience > 19
		}
		custom_cost_text = air_xp_20

		visible = {
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				NOT = {
					original_tag = USA #United States
					original_tag = CHI
					original_tag = FRA
					original_tag = GER
					original_tag = ENG
					original_tag = SOV

					original_tag = SPR

					original_tag = PER
					original_tag = TUR
					original_tag = EGY
					original_tag = SAU
					original_tag = SWE
					original_tag = BRA
					has_country_flag = USoE
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = gen_4_light
		}

		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision generic_gen_4_large_upgrade_1"
			#air_experience = -1
			create_equipment_variant = { #Light Fighter
				name = "Gen 4 Light Multirole Fighter"
				type = small_plane_strike_airframe_2
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_main_weapon_slot = weap_mp_med_hardpoint_1
					fixed_gun_slot = weap_multi_gun_2
					fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = weap_a2a_hardpoint_1
					engine_type_slot = engine_light_single_2
					avionics_type_slot = avionics_manned_2
					wingform_type_slot = wing_delta
					special_slot_type_1 = spec_countermeasures_2
					special_slot_type_2 = spec_tgp_1
					special_slot_type_3 = spec_refuel_3
				}
				upgrades = {
				}
				icon = "gfx/interface/technologies/ENG/AIR/INT.dds"				
			}
		}		

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 999
		}
	}

		days_remove = -1
		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			#has_air_experience > 19
		}
		custom_cost_text = air_xp_20

		visible = {
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				original_tag = ISR
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_tech = gen_5_large
			has_tech = engines_3
			has_tech = awacs_3
			has_tech = countermeasures_3
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision isr_gen_5_awacs"
			#air_experience = -20
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "G660 CAEW"
				type = large_plane_awacs_airframe_3
				modules = {
					fixed_main_weapon_slot = weap_buff_awacs_3
					engine_type_slot = engine_jet_double_3
					avionics_type_slot = avionics_manned_4
					wingform_type_slot = wing_swept
					special_slot_type_1 = spec_countermeasures_3
					special_slot_type_2 = spec_redundant_3
					special_slot_type_4 = spec_refuel_3
					special_slot_type_3 = spec_protection_3
				}
				upgrades = {
					plane_bba_engine_upgrade = 0
					plane_bba_radar_upgrade = 5
				}
				design_team = mio:ISR_israel_aerospace_industries_aircraft_manufacturer		
			}		
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 999
		}
	}
